PS>CommandInvocation(Get-Help): "Get-Help"
>> ParameterBinding(Get-Help): name="Name"; value="Write-VSCodeHtmlContentView"
>> ParameterBinding(Get-Help): name="Online"; value="False"
>> ParameterBinding(Get-Help): name="ErrorAction"; value="Ignore"

NAME
    Write-VSCodeHtmlContentView

SYNOPSIS
    Writes an HTML fragment to an HtmlContentView.


SYNTAX
    Write-VSCodeHtmlContentView [-HtmlContentView] <IHtmlContentView> [-AppendedHtmlBodyContent] <String> [<CommonParameters>]


DESCRIPTION
    Writes an HTML fragment to an HtmlContentView.  This new fragment is appended to the existing content, useful in cases where the output will
    be appended to an ongoing output stream.


RELATED LINKS

REMARKS
    To see the examples, type: "Get-Help Write-VSCodeHtmlContentView -Examples"
    For more information, type: "Get-Help Write-VSCodeHtmlContentView -Detailed"
    For technical information, type: "Get-Help Write-VSCodeHtmlContentView -Full"
